# E2R Stock-Web Historical Calibration / Sector-Archetype Residual Research Round

## 0. Research Metadata

```text

output_file = e2r_stock_web_v12_residual_round_R13_loop_13_L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC_R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM_research.md
price_source = Songdaiki/stock-web
stock_web_manifest_max_date = 2026-02-20
```

This loop adds **47** new cross-pattern representative cases, **30** representative counterexamples/residual rows, and **47** total trigger-level current-profile residual errors for **R13 / L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC / R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM**.

R13 is the circuit breaker room. It does not create another sector story. It takes the completed R1~R12 loop 13 rooms and asks whether the same short-circuit appears across them: price-only promotion, high-MAE false positives, local 4B mistaken for full-cycle exit, hard 4C too early/late, and the opposite risk of blocking clean structural winners.

## 1. Current Calibrated Profile Assumption

```text
current_default_profile_proxy = e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated_proxy
previous_baseline_reference = e2r_2_0_baseline_reference
stage2_actionable_evidence_bonus = +2.0
stage3_yellow_total_min = 75.0
stage3_green_total_min = 87.0
stage3_green_revision_min = 55.0
stage3_cross_evidence_green_buffer = +1.5
price_only_blowoff_blocks_positive_stage = true
full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence = true
hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c = true
```

This file does not re-propose those global axes. It stress-tests whether loop 13 evidence requires a **cross-archetype router** around them: positive-stage promotion needs a durable non-price bridge; local price-only peaks stay as 4B overlay; full 4B needs non-price deterioration; hard 4C needs explicit thesis-break evidence; high-MAE structural winners must not be thrown out merely because the path was ugly.

The same stock rows are reused because R13 is not a new sector discovery pass. The new evidence is the cross-archetype compression: the same failure modes repeat across unrelated canonical archetypes.

## 6. Canonical Archetype Compression Map

The loop 13 source archetypes compress into five R13 residual buckets:

| cross_pattern_bucket | representative_count | all_trigger_count | avg_MFE90 | avg_MAE90 | cross_router_verdict |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---|
| clean_structural_holdout | 14 | 15 | 112.12 | -7.37 | promote only with non-price bridge |
| hard_4c_or_4b_4c_boundary | 14 | 22 | 35.91 | -28.47 | block or route to risk overlay/thesis break |
| 4b_overlay_timing | 10 | 26 | 97.3 | -18.97 | block or route to risk overlay/thesis break |
| missed_or_late_structural | 5 | 7 | 150.99 | -9.86 | promote only with non-price bridge |
| positive_stage_false_positive | 3 | 3 | 37.22 | -23.53 | block or route to risk overlay/thesis break |
| high_mae_structural_survivor | 1 | 1 | 59.46 | -27.07 | promote only with non-price bridge |

Mechanism: a headline is the match, but the earnings bridge is the wick. R13 only lets a Stage2/3 candle burn when the wick exists; otherwise the same flame is logged as 4B-local, watch, or 4C protection depending on the non-price evidence.

## 8. Positive vs Counterexample Balance

```text
representative_case_count = 47
positive_case_count = 17
counterexample_count = 30
calibration_usable_trigger_count = 74
4B_case_count = 46
4C_case_count = 22
current_profile_error_count = 47
```

The average return profile is deceptively strong: representative rows average **84.5% MFE90** and **114.31% MFE180**, but the same basket also averages **-17.84% MAE90** and **-23.97% MAE180**. R13 therefore treats raw upside as insufficient. The shape of the bridge matters.

## 9. Evidence Source Map

Evidence is inherited from the source MD rows and remains separated by stage:

```text
Stage2 evidence = public_event_or_disclosure / customer_or_order_quality / relative_strength / capacity_or_volume_route / policy_or_regulatory_optionality / backlog_or_delivery_visibility / early_revision_signal
Stage3 evidence = confirmed_revision / margin_bridge / multiple_public_sources / financial_visibility / repeat_order_or_conversion / durable_customer_confirmation / low_red_team_risk
4B evidence = valuation_blowoff / positioning_overheat / dilution_or_cb / capital_raise_or_overhang / contract_delay / legal_or_regulatory_block / margin_or_backlog_slowdown / explicit_event_cap / price_only_local_peak
4C evidence = contract_cancelled / call_off_or_order_cut / qualification_failure / regulatory_rejection / accounting_or_trust_break / forced_liquidation_or_crash / thesis_evidence_broken
```

R13 conclusion: price action can locate stress, but cannot by itself manufacture Stage2/3 evidence. The same is true in reverse: high MAE can signal risk, but cannot by itself erase a clean structural thesis.

## 13. Current Calibrated Profile Stress Test

Current profile verdict distribution over representative rows:

```text
current_profile_4B_too_late = 1
current_profile_4C_too_early = 1
current_profile_4C_too_late = 2
current_profile_correct = 19
current_profile_false_positive = 18
current_profile_missed_structural = 2
current_profile_too_early = 1
current_profile_too_late = 3
```

Stress-test answers:

1. The current calibrated profile correctly blocks many price-only and headline-only rows, but not all of them.
2. The profile is still too early in some rows where the event was real but the non-price bridge was not yet investable.
3. The Stage2 actionable bonus is not globally wrong; it is too blunt when the event lacks direct transmission quality.
4. Yellow 75 and Green 87 work better after the non-price bridge gate; without the gate, high headline scores still become false positives.
5. Green revision minimum is kept; the residual is not threshold height alone but whether revision evidence is durable and route-specific.
6. The price-only blowoff guard is strengthened, not weakened.
7. Full 4B non-price requirement is strengthened: local price peaks remain overlay-only unless deterioration appears.
8. Hard 4C routing is kept but made sharper: ordinary MAE is not thesis break; explicit cancellation, failure, trust break, or route collapse is thesis break.

## 14. Stage2 / Yellow / Green Comparison

Stage2 rows with a durable bridge produced the best cross-archetype alignment. Stage3/Green labels were late when they waited for fully visible numbers after the MFE had already expanded. However, low-evidence Stage2 labels created the false-positive tail.

```text
Stage2 useful condition = non_price_bridge_exists AND route_specific_transmission_quality >= medium
Stage2 dangerous condition = headline_only OR price_only OR theme_proxy_without_customer/order/revision bridge
Yellow/Green useful condition = revision/margin bridge confirmed without thesis-break evidence
Yellow/Green dangerous condition = high valuation score plus weak bridge, especially after a local peak
```

## 15. 4B Local vs Full-window Timing Audit

```text
4B_trigger_count = 46
avg_four_b_local_peak_proximity = 0.79
avg_four_b_full_window_peak_proximity = 0.75
```

R13 keeps the split between local and full-window 4B. A local peak with no non-price deterioration is like a smoke alarm in one room: useful, but not the same as declaring the whole building condemned. Full 4B needs valuation/positioning heat plus some non-price reason that the thesis is capped or deteriorating.

## 16. 4C Protection Audit

```text
4C_trigger_count = 22
4C_rule = thesis_evidence_broken_or_trust_break_required
ordinary_high_MAE_is_not_4C = true
```

R10 and several event/biotech/platform rows show that 4C is protective when there is a hard thesis break. But GS건설-like boundary rows show the opposite error: a drawdown or PF headline can be a 4B/4C watch state before it is a full thesis break. The router therefore separates **watch**, **overlay**, and **hard 4C**.

## 17. Sector-Specific Rule Candidate

```text
sector_specific_rule_candidate = false
reason = R13 is not a sector rule file
```

Any sector-specific deltas remain in R1~R12 source files.

## 18. Canonical-Archetype Rule Candidate

```text
canonical_archetype_rule_candidate = true
canonical_scope = R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM
new_axis_proposed = NON_PRICE_BRIDGE_REQUIRED_FOR_POSITIVE_STAGE | LOCAL_4B_OVERLAY_NOT_FULL_EXIT | HARD_4C_THESIS_BREAK_ROUTER | HIGH_MAE_STRUCTURAL_SURVIVOR_EXCEPTION
```

Rule candidate:

```text
if positive_stage_candidate and price_or_headline_only:
    block Stage2/Stage3 promotion
    route to watch or local_4B_overlay

if positive_stage_candidate and durable non-price bridge exists:
    allow Stage2/Yellow/Green according to current thresholds

if MAE is high but non-price bridge remains intact:
    do not hard-route to 4C
    mark high_MAE_structural_survivor and require sizing/risk overlay

if explicit thesis break, cancellation, qualification failure, trust break, or route collapse exists:
    allow hard 4C thesis-break routing
```

## 23. Validation Scope / Non-Validation Scope

Validated:

```text
- R1~R12 loop13 source rows already carry Stock-Web OHLC entry/forward metrics.
- R13 reuses those rows for cross-archetype guardrail validation.
- No live candidate scan was performed.
- No stock_agent production code was opened or patched.
- No production scoring changed.
```

Not validated:

```text
- This file does not prove a new global production rule by itself.
- This file does not recommend any current security.
- This file does not use broker/order/live data.
- This file does not alter stock_agent source code.
```

## 24. Shadow Weight Calibration

The shadow rows below are cross-archetype ledger candidates only. They are designed to be ingested later and aggregated with other R13 checkpoints before any production promotion.

```text
proposal_type = cross_archetype_shadow_only
production_scoring_changed = false
confidence = medium
main_effect = reduce false positives without deleting high-MAE structural successes
```

## 25. Machine-Readable Rows

## 26. Deferred Coding Agent Handoff Prompt

### Purpose

You are now in the repository implementation phase. The attached Markdown files are v12 post-calibrated residual research outputs produced using the Songdaiki/stock-web OHLC atlas.

These MDs are not live candidate research. They are historical calibration research designed to extend the already-applied e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated profile.

Do not blindly apply every shadow row. Ingest the machine-readable rows and update the sector/canonical-archetype calibration ledger.

### Price source context

- Primary historical price source used by the research MD: Songdaiki/stock-web.
- Price basis: tradable_raw.
- Price adjustment status: raw_unadjusted_marcap.
- Price shard pattern: atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year/<prefix>/<ticker>/<year>.csv.
- Symbol profile pattern: atlas/symbol_profiles/<prefix>/<ticker>.json.

### Rules

- Use only calibration_usable=true rows for quantitative calibration.
- Do not count reused cases as new sector evidence unless independent_evidence_weight > 0 and the row is explicitly an R13 cross-pattern validation row.
- Do not treat schema_rematerialization_only or duplicate_low_value_loop as new evidence.
- Do not apply global deltas unless multiple large_sector_id values support the same direction.
- Prefer sector_specific or canonical_archetype_specific shadow profiles.
- Positive score promotion requires non-price evidence and clean 180D MFE/MAE.
- 4B rows are overlay/risk calibration only.
- 4C rows are thesis-break/protection calibration only.
- price-only rows cannot promote Stage2/Stage3.
- If a v12 MD weakens an already applied axis, log it as residual counterexample rather than immediately reverting.
- Production scoring must not change unless the user explicitly asks for another promotion batch.

### Expected repository tasks

1. Parse case / trigger / score_simulation / shadow_weight / residual_contribution rows.
2. Validate stock-web price source fields.
3. Validate large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
4. Validate novelty and reuse fields.
5. Deduplicate same_entry_group_id and reused cases.
6. Aggregate by large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
7. Update sector_shadow_profile and archetype_shadow_profile only.
8. Preserve global calibrated profile unless explicitly promoted.
9. Report new independent cases, counterexamples, and residual error types.
10. Add tests that duplicate low-value loops cannot change weights.

### Expected output

- Concise implementation summary.
- Rows accepted/rejected.
- New sector/canonical archetype coverage.
- Existing axis strengthened/weakened/kept.
- No investment recommendation language.

```text

```

Stock-Web manifest facts used here: source is FinanceData/marcap, raw/unadjusted OHLC, max date 2026-02-20, 14,354,401 tradable rows, 15,214,118 raw rows, 5,414 symbols, and markets KONEX/KOSDAQ/KOSDAQ GLOBAL/KOSPI. The schema confirms tradable columns `d,o,h,l,c,v,a,mc,s,m`, raw rows add `rs`, and calibration requires valid positive OHLCV, 180 forward tradable days, computed MFE/MAE, and clean corporate-action windows.
